--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View SALES_MOVIE
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "PROJECT1"."SALES_MOVIE" ("MOVIENO", "MOVIENAME", "PRICE") AS 
  SELECT MV.MOVIENO, MV.MOVIENAME, TK.PRICE
FROM MOVIE MV, TICKETING TK
WHERE MV.MOVIENO = tk.movieno
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View SHOW_BOOKED_SEAT
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "PROJECT1"."SHOW_BOOKED_SEAT" ("MOVIENO", "MOVIENAME", "BOOKING_DATE", "SEAT") AS 
  SELECT DISTINCT MV.MOVIENO, MV.MOVIENAME, BS.BOOKING_DATE, (S.SEATROW||S.SEATCOLUMN) AS SEAT
FROM BOOKING_SEAT BS, MOVIE MV, TIME TM, THEATER TH, SEAT S
WHERE BS.TIMENO = TM.TIMENO
AND TM.THEATERNO = TM.THEATERNO
AND MV.MOVIENO = TH.MOVIENO
AND BS.SEATNO = S.SEATNO
ORDER BY MOVIENO, BOOKING_DATE DESC, SEAT
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View SHOW_SALES
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "PROJECT1"."SHOW_SALES" ("MOVIENO", "MOVIENAME", "BOOKING_DATE", "PAYTYPE", "PRICE") AS 
  SELECT DISTINCT MV.MOVIENO, MV.MOVIENAME, BS.BOOKING_DATE, BK.PAYTYPE, BK.PRICE
FROM BOOKING_SEAT BS, TIME TM, THEATER TH, MOVIE MV, BANK BK
WHERE BK.ORDER_DATE = BS.BOOKING_DATE
AND BS.TIMENO = tm.timeno
AND TM.THEATERNO = TH.THEATERNO
AND TH.MOVIENO = MV.MOVIENO
ORDER BY MOVIENO, BOOKING_DATE DESC, PAYTYPE, PRICE
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View THEATER_VIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "PROJECT1"."THEATER_VIEW" ("THEATERNO", "NAME", "LOCATION", "SPECIAL", "MOVIENO") AS 
  SELECT T."THEATERNO",T."NAME",T."LOCATION",T."SPECIAL",T."MOVIENO"
FROM MOVIE M, THEATER T
WHERE M.MOVIENO = T.MOVIENO
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View TICKET_VIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "PROJECT1"."TICKET_VIEW" ("TICKETINGNO", "NAME", "SEATROW", "SEATCOLUMN", "MOVIENAME", "MOVIERATING", "MEMBERID", "STARTTIME", "ENDTIME") AS 
  SELECT tk.ticketingno, TH.NAME, S.SEATROW, S.SEATCOLUMN, M.MOVIENAME, M.MOVIERATING, MI.MEMBERID, t.starttime, t.endtime
FROM TICKETING TK, THEATER TH, SEAT S, MOVIE M ,MEMBER MI, TIME T
WHERE TK.THEATERNO = TH.THEATERNO
AND TK.SEATNO = S.SEATNO
and tk.movieno = m.movieno
and tk.memberid = MI.MEMBERID
AND TK.TIMENO = T.TIMENO
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View TIMENO_VIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "PROJECT1"."TIMENO_VIEW" ("TIMENO", "STARTTIME", "ENDTIME", "NAME") AS 
  SELECT T.TIMENO, T.STARTTIME, T.ENDTIME, TH.NAME
FROM TIME T, THEATER TH
WHERE T.THEATERNO = TH.THEATERNO
;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View TIME_VIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "PROJECT1"."TIME_VIEW" ("TIMENO", "STARTTIME", "ENDTIME", "THEATERNO") AS 
  SELECT T."TIMENO",T."STARTTIME",T."ENDTIME",T."THEATERNO"
FROM TIME T, THEATER TH
WHERE T.THEATERNO = TH.THEATERNO
;
